<h4 class="testimonial-content__title">Joyous Learning is a learning centre that really cares for their students.</h4>

<p class="testimonial-contect__description">Joyous Learning is a learning centre that really cares for their students. A big thank you to Adrian and his team for putting in their heart into helping my son with his PSLE prep. The weekly online tuition sessions were very useful for helping him to catch up with "lost time" that enabled him to gain confidence in facing the psle. The curriculum and materials of the centre are well organised and paced very well for PSLE preparation. The centre manager Irah was also always ready to support during the online lesson times. 												<a class="elementor-toggle-title" tabindex="0">1. What are the qualifications of the teachers?</a>
					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2131" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="1" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2131"><p>With the exception of the Dean, all our teachers are former/current MOE primary/ secondary school teachers with decades of experience. In addition to being highly conversant with school syllabi and examination (PSLE/O-Level/IP/IB) requirements, our teachers are equipped with the skills to guide students with different learning profiles.</p></div>

					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2137" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="7" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2137"><p>All classes commence on the first week of January and end on the last week of November with the exception of</p><ul><li>P6 programmes: end 1 week prior to the corresponding PSLE subject</li><li>P3 GEP Selection Preparation: ends 1 week prior to the GEP Selection Test (in mid-October)</li><li>S4 English: end 1 week prior to the O-Level English paper</li></ul><p>There are no classes in December.</p></div>

The fee for the month is prorated accordingly if the student joins after the first lesson of the month.</p></div>

					</div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-2139" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="9" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-2139"><p>A student can join another class of the same subject within the same week (starting on Monday and ending on Sunday) as long as there is a seat if the replacement class.<br><br>Alternative, the teacher can record the lesson for the student to view at a later time.</p></div>

					<div id="elementor-tab-content-21310" class="elementor-tab-content elementor-clearfix" data-tab="10" role="region" aria-labelledby="elementor-tab-title-21310"><p>Replacement classes are arranged for lessons affected by public holidays. The dates and timings for the replacement classes will be communicated to students and parents with due notice.</p></div>

<script>
	jQuery(document).ready(function($){
		$(".schedule-table .schedule-table-tab .elementor-widget-button").on("click", function(){
			const selectedTab = $(this).attr("data-table");
			$(".schedule-table .schedule-table-tab .elementor-widget-button").removeClass("tab-active");
			$(this).addClass("tab-active");
			$(".schedule-table .schedule-table-content").fadeOut();
			$("#schedule-table-" + selectedTab).fadeIn();
		});
	});
</script>
